<script type="text/javascript">
  var IsSubscriptionBottomWork = false;
  function sendSubscriptionBottom() {
    if( !IsSubscriptionBottomWork ) {
			var plhs = $('.form .kr_placeholder');
			plhs.each(function() {
				var input = $(this);
				var plh = input.attr('placeholder');
				if(plh == input.val()) {
					input.val('').removeClass('kr_placeholder_active');
				}
			});
			
      var txt = $('#subscriptionbottom').html();
      //$('#subscriptionbottom a').addClass('sbactive');
      $('#subscriptionbottom').html('Подождите...');
      IsSubscriptionBottomWork = true;
      $.get('/bitrix/components/pitcom/subscription/ajax.php',
        { 
          type: 'subscription',
          name: $('#subscriptionbottomname').val(),
          email: $('#subscriptionbottomemail').val()
        }, 
        function(data) {
          if( data.substr(0,6) == '+INFO:' ) {
            alert(data.substr(6));
            $('#subscriptionbottomname').val('');
            $('#subscriptionbottomemail').val('');
          }else
          if( data.substr(0,5) == '-ERR:' ) {
            alert('Ошибка подписки'+"\n\n"+data.substr(5));
          }else
          if( data == '+OK' ) {
            //alert('Вы успешно подписались на рассылку.');
			
			window.location.href = '/subscription_result/';	//перенаправляем на страницу
            //$('#subscriptionbottom').hide();
          }else{
            alert(data);
          }
          IsSubscriptionBottomWork = false;

<script>
	function bodyEvent(func) {
		var codes = [].slice.call(arguments, 1);
		var pressed = {};
		
		document.onkeydown = function(e) {
			e = e || window.event;

			pressed[e.keyCode] = true;

			for (var i = 0; i < codes.length; i++) {
				if (!pressed[codes[i]]) {
					return;
				}
			}

			pressed = {};

			func();
		};

		document.onkeyup = function(e) {
			e = e || window.event;
			delete pressed[e.keyCode];
		};
	}
		
		
	function closeModalWindow() {
		/*
		var modalWin = document.getElementById("modal-window-home-id");
		modalWin.style.display = "none";
		modalWin.parentNode.removeChild(modalWin);
		*/

		var modal = $('#modal-window-home-id');
		modal.removeClass('open');
		$('.content-modal-window', modal).html('');
	}
		
		
	function modalWindow() {
		var modal = $('#modal-window-home-id');
		if(modal.length > 0) {
			var text = '';
			var text_selected = copySelectionText();
			if(String(text_selected)) {
				var str = '';
				if(String(text_selected).length >= 120) {
					str = '...';
				}
				text = String(text_selected).substring(0, 120) + str;
			}
			
			var data = {
				ajax: true,
				task: 'show_error_feedback',
				error_message: text,
				error_url: String(window.location),
				error_referer: String(document.referrer),
				error_useragent: String(navigator.userAgent)
			}
			
			$.ajax({
				type: 'POST',
				async: false,
				url: '/tools/ajax.php',
				cache: false,
				data: data,
				dataType: 'json'
			}).done(function(answer) {
				if(answer.status == 'ok') {
					$('.content-modal-window', modal).html(answer.content);
					modal.addClass('open');
				}
			});
		}

	bodyEvent(modalWindow,"17","13");

	function modalWindowEsc(e) {
		if(e.keyCode == 27) {
			closeModalWindow();
		}
	}	
		
	addEventListener("keydown", modalWindowEsc);

	function handlerEvents(e) {
		var flagObjHandler = e.target.hasAttribute('data-params');
		if(flagObjHandler) {
			var objHandler = e.target.getAttribute('data-params');
			switch(objHandler) {
				case 'close':
					closeModalWindow();
					break;
			}
		}
	}


	window.onload = function() {
		document.body.addEventListener('click', handlerEvents);
	}

	function copySelectionText() {
		if(window.getSelection)
			strText = window.getSelection();
		else if(document.getSelection)
			strText = document.getSelection();
		else if(document.selection)
			strText = document.CDATA_SECTION_NODE.createRange().text;
		else return;

		return strText;
	}
